<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 3 <= a - 1; // Since a = n * 9 >= 9, we have a - 1 >= 8 >= 3
  assert a % 3 == 0; // Since a = n * 9, a is divisible by 3
  assert IsComposite(a);
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 3 <= b - 1; // Since b = n * 8 >= 8, we have b - 1 >= 7 >= 3
  assert b % 3 == 0; // Since b = n * 8, b is divisible by 3 when n >= 1
  assert IsComposite(b);
}

ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 9 && 9 <= a - 1; // Since a = n * 9 and n >= 1, we have a >= 9
  assert a % 9 == 0;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 8 && 8 <= b - 1; // Since b = n * 8 and n >= 1, we have b >= 8
  assert b % 8 == 0;

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 3 <= a - 1; // Since a = n*9 >= 9, we have a-1 >= 8 >= 3
  assert a % 3 == 0; // Since a = n*9, a is divisible by 3
  assert IsComposite(a);
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 3 <= b - 1; // Since b = n*8 >= 8, we have b-1 >= 7 >= 3
  assert b % 3 == 0; // Since b = n*8, b is divisible by 3 when n >= 1
  assert IsComposite(b);
}

ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 9 <= a - 1; // Since a = n * 9 and n >= 1, we have a >= 9
  assert a % 9 == 0;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 8 <= b - 1; // Since b = n * 8 and n >= 1, we have b >= 8
  assert b % 8 == 0;
}

ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 9 <= a - 1; // Since a = n * 9 and n >= 1, we have a >= 9
  assert a % 9 == 0;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 8 <= b - 1; // Since b = n * 8 and n >= 1, we have b >= 8
  assert b % 8 == 0;
}

<DAFNY_CODE>
ghost predicate IsComposite(x: int)
{
  x > 1 && exists d | 2 <= d <= x - 1 :: x % d == 0
}

method Equation(n: int) returns (a: int, b: int)
  requires n >= 1
  ensures IsComposite(a)
  ensures IsComposite(b)
  ensures a - b == n
{
  a := n * 9;
  b := n * 8;
  
  assert a - b == n;
  assert a > 1;
  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 2 <= 9 <= a - 1; // Since a = n * 9 and n >= 1, we have a >= 9
  assert a % 9 == 0;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= 8 <= b - 1; // Since b = n * 8 and n >= 1, we have b >= 8
  assert b % 8 == 0;
}

  assert b > 1;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(a)
  assert 3 <= a && a % 3 == 0;
  assert exists d | 2 <= d <= a - 1 :: a % d == 0;
  
  // Prove IsComposite(b)
  assert 2 <= b && b % 2 == 0;
  assert exists d | 2 <= d <= b - 1 :: b % d == 0;
}



--- DAFNY OUTPUT ---
Dafny program verifier finished with 2 verified, 0 errors
